		<div class="component_area parsys_c1"><div class="mds-area-pn1"><div class="parbase cnt_hl_c2 section"><div class="mod modCnt_hl_2 mds-cmp-content07 cnt_hl_2">
	<h2 class="hl_t ">
					2014 Camaro, Corvette Stingray and SS Sedan Take Center Stage</h2>
			</div></div>
</div><div class="mds-area-pn1"><div class="modCnt_par_1 mod cnt_par_1 section mds-cmp-content01"><h3  class="pt">
			</h3>
		<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
				<p>  The New York International Auto Show will host the world debut of the revamped 2014 Camaro. This newest edition advances the design and performance attributes that have made Camaro the most popular sports car under $50,000 for three consecutive years. </p>
<p>  In an impressive four-car display of advanced performance technology, the restyled Camaro will be unveiled alongside the all-new Corvette Stingray convertible, the all-new Corvette Stingray coupe, and the 415-hp Chevrolet SS sedan.</p>
<p>  Be sure to watch the live reveal of the new Camaro here on March 27.</p></div>
		</div>
</div><div class="mds-area-pn1"><div class="section mm_c1"><div class="mds-cmp-content05 mm_1 mod modMm_1" id="">
	<iframe id="5qVWNxvV_Yw" name="mmpar_yt_video" title="Chevrolet Camaro" class="youtube-player" type="text/html" src="//www.youtube.com/embed/5qVWNxvV_Yw?rel=0&amp;wmode=transparent&amp;enablejsapi=1&amp;id=5qVWNxvV_Yw"  width="648" height="360" frameborder="0" >
Your browser does not support iframes.
</iframe>
</div>
</div>
</div><div class="mds-area-pn1"><div class="section mm_c1"><div class="mds-cmp-content05 mm_1 mod modMm_1" id="">
	<div class="mm_scroll ui_navigation_img">
			<span class="prev"></span><ul>
				<li class="mm_mos_1_item" id="">
						<div class="mod modMm_imagevideo_1"><figure >			
			<img src="/content/dam/Chevrolet/northamerica/usa/nscwebsite/en/Home/Chevy%20Culture/News/NYAS/01-images/2013-culture-news-ny-auto-show-mm-1-1-648x316.jpg" alt="" width="648" height="316" class="mm"/></figure>	
	</div>
</li>
				<li class="mm_mos_1_item" id="">
						<div class="mod modMm_imagevideo_1"><figure >

	<dl style="width:316px" class="figure" >
					<dd>
									<img src="/content/dam/Chevrolet/northamerica/usa/nscwebsite/en/Home/Chevy%20Culture/News/NYAS/01-images/2013-culture-news-ny-auto-show-mm-2-1-316x137.jpg" alt="Corvette Stingray at New York International Auto Show" title="Corvette Stingray at New York International Auto Show" width="316" height="137"/></dd>

								</dl>
			<div class="text " id="">
				<h3 class="pt">
						Corvette Stingray Convertible Makes American Debut</h3>
				<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
						<p>After a rousing global reveal earlier this month at the Geneva Motor Show, the all-new 2014 <a href="/culture/article/stingray-convertible-unveiling.html" onclick="if(typeof(Omniture_s) != 'undefined'){mrm.util.tagging.omniture_tl(this, this.href, 'o', undefined, {'prop27':'contentarea'});}">Corvette Stingray convertible</a> rolls into the Big Apple. “The Corvette Stingray offers an open-top driving experience with no compromise in performance, technology or design,” says Ed Welburn, GM vice president of global design. The Corvette Stingray convertible will be available fourth quarter 2013.</p></div>
				</div>
		</div></div>
</div><div class="mds-area-pn1"><div class="modCnt_par_1 mod cnt_par_1 section mds-cmp-content01"><h3  class="pt">
			Corvette Stingray Coupe Redefines Modern Performance</h3>
		<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
				<p>Only a Corvette with the perfect balance of technology, design and performance can wear the iconic Stingray designation. The <a href="/one13thirteen.html" onclick="if(typeof(Omniture_s) != 'undefined'){mrm.util.tagging.omniture_tl(this, this.href, 'o', undefined, {'prop27':'contentarea'});}">Stingray</a>&nbsp; lives up to its legacy with an all-new frame structure and chassis, a new powertrain and supporting technologies, as well as an all-new interior and exterior. The Corvette Stingray coupe will be available late Summer 2013.</p></div>
		</div>
</div><div class="mds-area-pn1"><div class="modCnt_par_1 mod cnt_par_1 section mds-cmp-content01"><h3  class="pt">
			All-New Chevrolet SS Sedan Delivers Performance with Elegance</h3>
		<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
				<p>Enthusiasts have reason to celebrate — the <a href="/culture/article/ss-performance-sedan-debut.html" onclick="if(typeof(Omniture_s) != 'undefined'){mrm.util.tagging.omniture_tl(this, this.href, 'o', undefined, {'prop27':'contentarea'});}">415-horsepower SS</a>&nbsp; is the first rear-wheel-drive Chevrolet sedan in 17 years. This high-performance 4-door SS will please knowledgeable enthusiasts who seek an exhilarating driving experience, plus the luxury, style and convenience features of a premium sedan. Additionally, with the introduction of the SS sedan, Chevrolet is the only manufacturer to offer the same rear-wheel drive V8 configuration in its production car as it does in its NASCAR Sprint Cup Series™ race car. The SS sedan will be available late 2013.</p>
<p>Join the conversation on <a href="http://twitter.com/#!/chevrolet" onclick="getOmnitureLinktrackingCode('http://twitter.com/#!/chevrolet');" class="dl_pdf" target="_blank">Twitter</a> and Facebook for <a href="http://www.facebook.com/corvette" onclick="getOmnitureLinktrackingCode('http://www.facebook.com/corvette');" class="ln_facebook" target="_blank">Corvette</a>, <a href="https://www.facebook.com/chevycamaro" onclick="getOmnitureLinktrackingCode('https://www.facebook.com/chevycamaro');" class="ln_facebook" target="_blank">Camaro</a> and <a href="http://www.facebook.com/chevrolet" onclick="getOmnitureLinktrackingCode('http://www.facebook.com/chevrolet');" class="ln_facebook" target="_blank">SS</a>.</p></div>
